**CHECKLIST 2 --- CONCRETE SLAB**

**Poly Injection / Slab Leveling**
==================================

Complete before building any slab leveling proposal

  --------------------------------------------------- ---------------------------------- ---------------------------------- -----------------------------------
  Rep: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Job Type: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Outcome: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_
  --------------------------------------------------- ---------------------------------- ---------------------------------- -----------------------------------

**Phase 1 --- Pre-Inspection**
------------------------------

+------------------------+--------------------------------------------+
| **SITE DOCUMENTATION** |                                            |
+========================+============================================+
| ☐                      | Photograph the settled slab from multiple  |
|                        | angles before any measurement              |
+------------------------+--------------------------------------------+
| ☐                      | Note water drainage patterns around the    |
|                        | settled slab                               |
|                        |                                            |
|                        | Gutters, downspouts, and surface slope --- |
|                        | the cause of erosion is usually visible    |
+------------------------+--------------------------------------------+
| ☐                      | Note any large trees within 15 feet of the |
|                        | slab                                       |
|                        |                                            |
|                        | Root systems can cause settlement or heave |
+------------------------+--------------------------------------------+
| ☐                      | Ask customer: when did this start, and did |
|                        | anything change around that time?          |
|                        |                                            |
|                        | Recent plumbing work, drought, flooding,   |
|                        | or construction are all diagnostic clues   |
+------------------------+--------------------------------------------+

**Phase 2 --- Slab Assessment**
-------------------------------

+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **DIFFERENTIAL       |                      |                      |
| MEASUREMENT**        |                      |                      |
+======================+======================+======================+
| ☐                    | Measure and record   |                      |
|                      | differential at the  |                      |
|                      | most pronounced      |                      |
|                      | point with a level   |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | 1" per 8 ft = flag   |                      |
|                      | \| 1/2" at a joint = |                      |
|                      | trip hazard \|       |                      |
|                      | document precisely   |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Probe the settled    |                      |
|                      | panel to estimate    |                      |
|                      | void size beneath    |                      |
|                      | the slab             |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Metal rod or probe   |                      |
|                      | can estimate void    |                      |
|                      | depth and lateral    |                      |
|                      | extent               |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Assess adjacent      |                      |
|                      | panels for related   |                      |
|                      | movement             |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Multiple panels may  |                      |
|                      | need attention ---   |                      |
|                      | scope each           |                      |
|                      | separately           |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **MEASUREMENT**      | **RECORDED VALUE**   | **REFERENCE /        |
|                      |                      | THRESHOLD**          |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Differential at    | \_\_                 | in. --- at 1"/8ft    |
| primary settled      | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | flag; 1/2"+ at a     |
| point**              |                      | joint = trip hazard  |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Differential at    | \_\_                 | in. --- trip hazard  |
| transition to        | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | at 1/2"+             |
| adjacent panel**     |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Estimated void     | \_\_                 | in. --- note if \>6" |
| depth (probe)**      | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | (may require         |
|                      |                      | pre-fill)            |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Estimated affected | \_\_                 | sq ft (for injection |
| area**               | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | hole placement       |
|                      |                      | planning)            |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **SLAB CONDITION     |                      |                      |
| ASSESSMENT**         |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Assess crack         |                      |
|                      | pattern: number,     |                      |
|                      | width, and direction |                      |
|                      | of cracks            |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Photograph all       |                      |
|                      | cracks before        |                      |
|                      | recommending lift    |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Assess slab        |                      |
|                      | integrity: is the    |                      |
|                      | concrete             |                      |
|                      | structurally         |                      |
|                      | sound?**             |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Severely crumbled,   |                      |
|                      | spalled, or          |                      |
|                      | multi-fractured      |                      |
|                      | slabs may require    |                      |
|                      | replacement          |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Check for rebar    |                      |
|                      | exposure or          |                      |
|                      | significant concrete |                      |
|                      | deterioration**      |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Exposed rebar = poly |                      |
|                      | injection may not be |                      |
|                      | appropriate for this |                      |
|                      | slab                 |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Assess tree root   |                      |
|                      | involvement**        |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Root heave requires  |                      |
|                      | root management;     |                      |
|                      | injection without    |                      |
|                      | addressing roots     |                      |
|                      | will re-fail         |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Check for evidence |                      |
|                      | of a plumbing leak   |                      |
|                      | beneath the slab**   |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Localized rapid      |                      |
|                      | settlement, floor    |                      |
|                      | drain issues, or wet |                      |
|                      | soil = evaluate      |                      |
|                      | plumbing first       |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Assess access and    |                      |
|                      | injection hole       |                      |
|                      | placement            |                      |
|                      | feasibility          |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Vehicles, equipment, |                      |
|                      | or obstacles over    |                      |
|                      | the slab that limit  |                      |
|                      | drill access must be |                      |
|                      | noted                |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **⚠ CRITICAL FLAG:** |                      |                      |
| If settlement is     |                      |                      |
| localized, rapid, or |                      |                      |
| follows a linear     |                      |                      |
| path suggesting a    |                      |                      |
| pipe route, evaluate |                      |                      |
| for a plumbing leak  |                      |                      |
| before proceeding.   |                      |                      |
| Injecting foam over  |                      |                      |
| an active leak masks |                      |                      |
| the problem and      |                      |                      |
| produces temporary   |                      |                      |
| results.             |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+

**Phase 3 --- Required Photos**
-------------------------------

  **✓**   **PHOTO SUBJECT**                                                         **STATUS**
  ------- ------------------------------------------------------------------------- --------------
  ☐       **Settled slab from multiple angles showing full extent of settlement**   **REQUIRED**
  ☐       **Tape measure or level showing the differential measurement**            **REQUIRED**
  ☐       **All cracks in the slab --- each one photographed separately**           **REQUIRED**
  ☐       **Adjacent panels for context**                                           **REQUIRED**
  ☐       Drainage paths near the slab (gutters, downspouts, surface slope)         if present
  ☐       Any root intrusion or relevant tree proximity                             if present
  ☐       Any evidence of plumbing leak (wet soil, staining, odor)                  if present

**Phase 4 --- Diagnostic Flags**
--------------------------------

+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| **EVALUATE BEFORE LEAVING THE    |                                  |
| SITE**                           |                                  |
+==================================+==================================+
| ☐                                | **Is the slab structurally sound |
|                                  | enough to be lifted as a unit?** |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Severely cracked or crumbled =   |
|                                  | replacement, not injection       |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | **Is a plumbing leak the likely  |
|                                  | cause of the settlement?**       |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Must be repaired before          |
|                                  | injection                        |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | **Are tree roots involved in the |
|                                  | settlement?**                    |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Root management must be part of  |
|                                  | the recommendation               |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Is the void deeper than 6--8     |
|                                  | inches?                          |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | May require pre-fill material    |
|                                  | before lift foam injection       |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Is the root cause of settlement  |
|                                  | identified and documented?       |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Every proposal should name the   |
|                                  | cause and recommend how to       |
|                                  | prevent recurrence               |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Has the patch hole appearance    |
|                                  | expectation been set with the    |
|                                  | customer?                        |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | 5/8" holes will be visible after |
|                                  | patching --- tell the customer   |
|                                  | before work begins, not after    |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| **INSPECTION SUMMARY**           |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Primary cause of settlement:     |                                  |
| water erosion / poor compaction  |                                  |
| / plumbing / roots / organic /   |                                  |
| unknown                          |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Differential at worst point:     |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\"   Void depth    |                                  |
| estimated: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\"      |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Slab condition: sound (liftable) |                                  |
| / compromised (evaluate for      |                                  |
| replacement)                     |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Plumbing leak suspected: yes     |                                  |
| (evaluate before proceeding) /   |                                  |
| no                               |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Scope recommendation:            |                                  |
| \_\_\_                           |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                                  |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+

**CHECKLIST 3 --- FOUNDATION**

**Structural Piers Inspection**
===============================

Complete before building any pier proposal

  --------------------------------------------------- ---------------------------------- ---------------------------------- -----------------------------------
  Rep: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Job Type: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Outcome: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_
  --------------------------------------------------- ---------------------------------- ---------------------------------- -----------------------------------

**Phase 1 --- Pre-Inspection**
------------------------------

+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| **SITE & CUSTOMER                |                                  |
| DOCUMENTATION**                  |                                  |
+==================================+==================================+
| ☐                                | Walk the full exterior perimeter |
|                                  | with the customer present        |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Observe and explain out loud --- |
|                                  | what you name first is what      |
|                                  | they'll remember                 |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Photograph all exterior crack    |
|                                  | patterns before taking any       |
|                                  | measurements                     |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Stair-step, diagonal, vertical,  |
|                                  | and horizontal --- each          |
|                                  | photographed separately          |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Note trees within 15--20 feet of |
|                                  | the settling area                |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Root desiccation is a common     |
|                                  | Panhandle cause of seasonal      |
|                                  | foundation movement              |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Ask customer: when symptoms      |
|                                  | first appeared, and whether      |
|                                  | they've changed                  |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Progression indicators help      |
|                                  | assess urgency and cause         |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Confirm footing type if          |
|                                  | possible: poured concrete,       |
|                                  | block, or brick                  |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Footing type determines push vs. |
|                                  | helical pier suitability         |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+

**Phase 2 --- Foundation Assessment**
-------------------------------------

+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **ELEVATION          |                      |                      |
| MAPPING**            |                      |                      |
+======================+======================+======================+
| ☐                    | Take floor elevation |                      |
|                      | measurements at      |                      |
|                      | multiple perimeter   |                      |
|                      | points               |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Note the lowest      |                      |
|                      | point and greatest   |                      |
|                      | differential across  |                      |
|                      | the structure        |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Record door and      |                      |
|                      | window frame         |                      |
|                      | squareness at        |                      |
|                      | affected areas       |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Out-of-square frames |                      |
|                      | confirm foundation   |                      |
|                      | has moved at that    |                      |
|                      | location             |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Measure floor slope  |                      |
|                      | at the most affected |                      |
|                      | interior area        |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | 1" per 8 ft =        |                      |
|                      | significant \| 2"+   |                      |
|                      | per 8 ft = urgent    |                      |
|                      | structural concern   |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **MEASUREMENT**      | **RECORDED VALUE**   | **REFERENCE /        |
|                      |                      | THRESHOLD**          |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Floor elevation    | \_\_                 | in. from reference   |
| --- corner A**       | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | datum:               |
|                      |                      | \_\_                 |
|                      |                      | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Floor elevation    | \_\_                 | in. from reference   |
| --- corner B**       | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | datum:               |
|                      |                      | \_\_                 |
|                      |                      | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Floor elevation    | \_\_                 | in. from reference   |
| --- corner C**       | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | datum:               |
|                      |                      | \_\_                 |
|                      |                      | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Floor elevation    | \_\_                 | in. from reference   |
| --- corner D**       | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | datum:               |
|                      |                      | \_\_                 |
|                      |                      | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Greatest           | \_\_                 | in. (1"/8 ft = flag  |
| differential**       | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | \| 2"+ = urgent)     |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Floor slope at     | \_\_                 | in. per 8 ft         |
| most affected area** | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **CRACK              |                      |                      |
| DOCUMENTATION**      |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Document all         |                      |
|                      | stair-step cracks in |                      |
|                      | brick or block       |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Note direction,      |                      |
|                      | width, and location  |                      |
|                      | --- photograph with  |                      |
|                      | coin for scale       |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Document diagonal    |                      |
|                      | cracks at door and   |                      |
|                      | window corners       |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Width at widest      |                      |
|                      | point; note if crack |                      |
|                      | is wider at top or   |                      |
|                      | bottom               |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Document vertical    |                      |
|                      | cracks in poured     |                      |
|                      | concrete foundation  |                      |
|                      | walls                |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Width and            |                      |
|                      | displacement at face |                      |
|                      | of crack             |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Check for and      |                      |
|                      | document horizontal  |                      |
|                      | cracks in block or   |                      |
|                      | concrete walls**     |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | HORIZONTAL = lateral |                      |
|                      | pressure, NOT        |                      |
|                      | settlement ---       |                      |
|                      | requires wall        |                      |
|                      | reinforcement        |                      |
|                      | evaluation           |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Note any bowing or |                      |
|                      | inward lean in       |                      |
|                      | foundation walls**   |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Wall reinforcement   |                      |
|                      | evaluation required  |                      |
|                      | in addition to any   |                      |
|                      | drainage or pier     |                      |
|                      | scope                |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Document gaps at     |                      |
|                      | wall-ceiling or      |                      |
|                      | wall-floor junctions |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Structural           |                      |
|                      | separation from      |                      |
|                      | differential         |                      |
|                      | settlement ---       |                      |
|                      | photograph from      |                      |
|                      | multiple angles      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Note doors sticking, |                      |
|                      | swinging open, or    |                      |
|                      | not closing square   |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Frame racking        |                      |
|                      | confirms foundation  |                      |
|                      | has moved at that    |                      |
|                      | location             |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Note window cracks   |                      |
|                      | or sticking          |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Corner cracks in     |                      |
|                      | glass confirm the    |                      |
|                      | frame has racked     |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **⚠ CRITICAL FLAG:** |                      |                      |
| Horizontal cracks in |                      |                      |
| a foundation wall    |                      |                      |
| indicate lateral     |                      |                      |
| soil pressure, not   |                      |                      |
| settlement. These    |                      |                      |
| require a wall       |                      |                      |
| reinforcement        |                      |                      |
| evaluation (wall     |                      |                      |
| anchors or carbon    |                      |                      |
| fiber). Never        |                      |                      |
| recommend piers      |                      |                      |
| alone for a          |                      |                      |
| horizontally         |                      |                      |
| cracking wall.       |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **SOIL & SITE        |                      |                      |
| CONDITIONS**         |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Assess drainage      |                      |
|                      | patterns around the  |                      |
|                      | settling area        |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Note soil type if    |                      |
|                      | visible at           |                      |
|                      | foundation (clay,    |                      |
|                      | sand, or             |                      |
|                      | organic-bearing)     |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Check for plumbing |                      |
|                      | leak evidence:       |                      |
|                      | localized            |                      |
|                      | settlement, wet soil |                      |
|                      | patches**            |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Plumbing evaluation  |                      |
|                      | may be warranted     |                      |
|                      | before pier          |                      |
|                      | installation         |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+

**Phase 3 --- Required Photos**
-------------------------------

  **✓**   **PHOTO SUBJECT**                                                         **STATUS**
  ------- ------------------------------------------------------------------------- --------------
  ☐       **Every crack pattern --- exterior and interior (with coin for scale)**   **REQUIRED**
  ☐       **Floor level showing differential (level tool visible)**                 **REQUIRED**
  ☐       **Door or window frame showing out-of-square condition**                  **REQUIRED**
  ☐       **Full foundation wall --- each side of structure**                       **REQUIRED**
  ☐       **Any horizontal cracking (structural flag)**                             **REQUIRED**
  ☐       **Any bowing or inward lean in walls**                                    **REQUIRED**
  ☐       Wall-ceiling or wall-floor separation if present                          if present
  ☐       Exterior grading and drainage patterns                                    if present

**Phase 4 --- Diagnostic Flags**
--------------------------------

+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| **EVALUATE BEFORE LEAVING THE    |                                  |
| SITE**                           |                                  |
+==================================+==================================+
| ☐                                | **Are horizontal cracks present? |
|                                  | (lateral pressure, not           |
|                                  | settlement)**                    |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Flag for wall reinforcement      |
|                                  | evaluation --- not a pier-only   |
|                                  | scope                            |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | **Is bowing or inward wall lean  |
|                                  | present?**                       |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Structural evaluation required   |
|                                  | before any other recommendation  |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | **Is the footing continuous and  |
|                                  | intact?**                        |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Cracked or discontinuous footing |
|                                  | = helical piers required, not    |
|                                  | push piers                       |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | **Is a plumbing leak a possible  |
|                                  | cause of the settlement?**       |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Localized rapid settlement in a  |
|                                  | linear pattern = evaluate        |
|                                  | plumbing                         |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Has pier type been determined:   |
|                                  | push or helical?                 |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Push = heavy structure with      |
|                                  | intact footing \| Helical =      |
|                                  | lighter or cracked footing       |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Have realistic lift expectations |
|                                  | been documented?                 |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Stabilization is the primary     |
|                                  | goal; lift is secondary and not  |
|                                  | guaranteed                       |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Has excavation disruption been   |
|                                  | disclosed to the customer?       |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Landscaping adjacent to the      |
|                                  | foundation will be disturbed --- |
|                                  | disclose before scheduling       |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| **INSPECTION SUMMARY**           |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Greatest differential:           |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\" at              |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                                  |
| \| Floor slope: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\" |                                  |
| per 8 ft                         |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Crack types present: stair-step  |                                  |
| / diagonal / vertical /          |                                  |
| horizontal / floor gaps          |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Horizontal cracking: yes (wall   |                                  |
| reinforcement eval required) /   |                                  |
| no                               |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Footing condition: continuous &  |                                  |
| intact / cracked or unknown ---  |                                  |
| Pier type: push / helical        |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Plumbing leak suspected: yes     |                                  |
| (evaluate before proceeding) /   |                                  |
| no                               |                                  |
|                                  |                                  |
| Scope recommendation:            |                                  |
| \_\_\_                           |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                                  |
| \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                                  |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+

**CHECKLIST 4 --- CRAWL SPACE**

**Drainage System Inspection**
==============================

Complete before building any crawl space drainage proposal

  --------------------------------------------------- ---------------------------------- ---------------------------------- -----------------------------------
  Rep: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Date: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Job Type: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_   Outcome: \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_
  --------------------------------------------------- ---------------------------------- ---------------------------------- -----------------------------------

**Phase 1 --- Pre-Inspection**
------------------------------

+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| **SITE & HISTORY DOCUMENTATION** |                                  |
+==================================+==================================+
| ☐                                | Walk exterior: assess grading,   |
|                                  | gutter condition, downspout      |
|                                  | discharge locations              |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Note any discharge point within  |
|                                  | 6 feet of the foundation         |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Ask customer: when does water    |
|                                  | appear --- seasonal or after     |
|                                  | specific rain events?            |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Seasonal = water table rising \| |
|                                  | After rain = surface or drainage |
|                                  | failure                          |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Ask customer: has drainage ever  |
|                                  | been installed? What previous    |
|                                  | work was done?                   |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Prior installations that failed  |
|                                  | are important diagnostic         |
|                                  | information                      |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Note any exterior French drain   |
|                                  | inlets, gravel beds, or drainage |
|                                  | features                         |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+
| ☐                                | Check for electrical outlet near |
|                                  | planned sump location            |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Dedicated circuit required ---   |
|                                  | note if electrical work will be  |
|                                  | needed before install            |
+----------------------------------+----------------------------------+

**Phase 2 --- Crawl Space Inspection**
--------------------------------------

+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **WATER SOURCE       |                      |                      |
| IDENTIFICATION**     |                      |                      |
+======================+======================+======================+
| ☐                    | Identify all water   |                      |
|                      | entry points: wall   |                      |
|                      | seams, footing-wall  |                      |
|                      | joint, floor seepage |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Photograph each      |                      |
|                      | entry point          |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Distinguish vapor  |                      |
|                      | from bulk water**    |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Standing water or    |                      |
|                      | staining = bulk      |                      |
|                      | water \| High        |                      |
|                      | humidity only =      |                      |
|                      | vapor /              |                      |
|                      | encapsulation        |                      |
|                      | problem              |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check for water      |                      |
|                      | staining on          |                      |
|                      | foundation walls,    |                      |
|                      | piers, and soil      |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Photograph all       |                      |
|                      | staining with enough |                      |
|                      | context to show      |                      |
|                      | location             |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check for            |                      |
|                      | efflorescence on     |                      |
|                      | block walls or piers |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | White mineral        |                      |
|                      | deposits = water has |                      |
|                      | been migrating       |                      |
|                      | through the wall     |                      |
|                      | repeatedly           |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check for silt       |                      |
|                      | deposits at base of  |                      |
|                      | walls                |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Silt = water has     |                      |
|                      | been flowing in and  |                      |
|                      | depositing sediment  |                      |
|                      | = bulk water entry   |                      |
|                      | confirmed            |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Measure water depth  |                      |
|                      | if standing water is |                      |
|                      | present              |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Identify the lowest  |                      |
|                      | point in the crawl   |                      |
|                      | space for sump       |                      |
|                      | placement            |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Note the specific    |                      |
|                      | location --- the     |                      |
|                      | sump must be at the  |                      |
|                      | absolute lowest      |                      |
|                      | elevation            |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **MEASUREMENT**      | **RECORDED VALUE**   | **REFERENCE /        |
|                      |                      | THRESHOLD**          |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Standing water     | \_\_                 | inches               |
| depth (if present)** | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Crawl space lowest | \_\_                 | location:            |
| elevation (approx    | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | \_\_\_\_\_\_         |
| location)**          |                      | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Approx crawl space | \_\_                 | linear feet (for     |
| perimeter**          | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | drain channel        |
|                      |                      | estimate)            |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **RH in crawl        | \_\_                 | Safe below 60% /     |
| space**              | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ | Problem above 60%    |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **EXISTING SYSTEM    |                      |                      |
| CONDITION**          |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Inspect existing     |                      |
|                      | sump pump:           |                      |
|                      | operational, float   |                      |
|                      | working, discharge   |                      |
|                      | intact?              |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Test by pouring      |                      |
|                      | water in the basin   |                      |
|                      | if accessible        |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+

|                      | perimeter drain      |                      |
|                      | channel condition if |                      |

|                      | clean-out ports      |                      |
|                      | present and          |                      |
|                      | accessible?          |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Inspect existing   |                      |
|                      | liner condition if   |                      |
|                      | present**            |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Is it floating,      |                      |
|                      | buckled, or showing  |                      |
|                      | signs of trapped     |                      |
|                      | water beneath?       |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Inspect discharge    |                      |
|                      | pipe endpoint        |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Must discharge 6+    |                      |
|                      | feet from foundation |                      |
|                      | on a path sloping    |                      |
|                      | permanently away     |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Note battery backup  |                      |
|                      | unit if present:     |                      |
|                      | age, test status     |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Recommend            |                      |
|                      | replacement if       |                      |
|                      | battery age is       |                      |
|                      | unknown or greater   |                      |
|                      | than 3 years         |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **⚠ CRITICAL FLAG:** |                      |                      |
| If a liner is        |                      |                      |
| present and the      |                      |                      |
| customer reports     |                      |                      |
| ongoing water        |                      |                      |
| issues, the liner    |                      |                      |
| may have been        |                      |                      |
| installed before     |                      |                      |
| drainage was         |                      |                      |
| addressed. Trapped   |                      |                      |
| water beneath a      |                      |                      |
| liner is a system    |                      |                      |
| failure. Evaluate    |                      |                      |
| before proposing     |                      |                      |
| additional           |                      |                      |
| encapsulation.       |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+

|                                  | why prior work failed            |

|                                  | drainage-before-encapsulation    |
|                                  | sequence been confirmed in the   |
|                                  | proposal?**                      |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Drainage always goes in first    |
|                                  | when both are needed             |

|                                  | downspouts, window wells         |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Note any discharge within 6 feet |
|                                  | of the foundation                |

| ☐                                | Ask customer: when does water    |
|                                  | appear --- seasonal, after rain, |
|                                  | or always?                       |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Seasonal = water table \| After  |
|                                  | rain = surface drainage failure  |

|                                  | tried before (coatings, crack    |
|                                  | injection, paint)?               |
|                                  |                                  |
|                                  | Prior failed solutions are       |
|                                  | diagnostic --- understand        |
|                                  | exactly what was done and when   |

**Phase 2 --- Basement Inspection**
-----------------------------------

+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **WATER ENTRY POINT  |                      |                      |
| IDENTIFICATION**     |                      |                      |
+======================+======================+======================+
| ☐                    | Check cove joint     |                      |
|                      | (wall-floor seam)    |                      |
|                      | for water entry or   |                      |
|                      | staining             |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | The most common      |                      |
|                      | entry point for      |                      |
|                      | hydrostatic pressure |                      |
|                      | --- photograph       |                      |
|                      | carefully            |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check all foundation |                      |
|                      | walls for uniform    |                      |
|                      | dampness or seepage  |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Even without cracks, |                      |
|                      | porous concrete      |                      |
|                      | transmits water      |                      |
|                      | under hydrostatic    |                      |
|                      | pressure             |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check for            |                      |
|                      | efflorescence on     |                      |
|                      | walls                |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | White mineral        |                      |
|                      | deposits = proof of  |                      |
|                      | repeated water       |                      |
|                      | movement through the |                      |
|                      | wall                 |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check floor slab for |                      |
|                      | seepage, cracks, or  |                      |
|                      | pooling away from    |                      |
|                      | walls                |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Floor seepage =      |                      |
|                      | water table has      |                      |
|                      | risen above floor    |                      |
|                      | level                |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check all window     |                      |
|                      | wells for drainage   |                      |
|                      | adequacy             |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Standing water in    |                      |
|                      | window wells = entry |                      |
|                      | point at frame or    |                      |
|                      | adjacent wall        |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check for and        |                      |
|                      | photograph all wall  |                      |
|                      | cracks               |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Note direction:      |                      |
|                      | vertical / diagonal  |                      |
|                      | / horizontal ---     |                      |
|                      | direction determines |                      |
|                      | cause                |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Check for          |                      |
|                      | horizontal wall      |                      |
|                      | cracks               |                      |
|                      | specifically**       |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | HORIZONTAL = lateral |                      |
|                      | soil pressure, not   |                      |
|                      | hydrostatic ---      |                      |
|                      | requires wall        |                      |
|                      | reinforcement eval   |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | **Check for bowing   |                      |
|                      | or inward lean in    |                      |
|                      | any wall**           |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Wall reinforcement   |                      |
|                      | evaluation required  |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **⚠ CRITICAL FLAG:** |                      |                      |
| Horizontal cracks in |                      |                      |
| a basement wall are  |                      |                      |
| caused by lateral    |                      |                      |
| soil pressure, not   |                      |                      |
| hydrostatic          |                      |                      |
| pressure. This is a  |                      |                      |
| structural issue     |                      |                      |
| requiring wall       |                      |                      |
| anchors or carbon    |                      |                      |
| fiber reinforcement  |                      |                      |
| in addition to       |                      |                      |
| drainage. Never      |                      |                      |
| propose drainage     |                      |                      |
| alone for a          |                      |                      |
| horizontally         |                      |                      |
| cracking wall.       |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **EXISTING SYSTEM    |                      |                      |
| CONDITION**          |                      |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Inspect existing     |                      |
|                      | sump pump:           |                      |
|                      | operational, float   |                      |
|                      | working, discharge   |                      |
|                      | intact?              |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Test by pouring      |                      |
|                      | water in basin if    |                      |
|                      | accessible           |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Inspect any existing |                      |
|                      | drain channel        |                      |
|                      | condition and slope  |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Is the channel       |                      |
|                      | actually connected   |                      |
|                      | to the sump and      |                      |
|                      | sloped toward it?    |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Inspect existing     |                      |
|                      | waterproofing        |                      |
|                      | coatings on walls    |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Bubbling, peeling,   |                      |
|                      | or delaminating      |                      |
|                      | coating = evidence   |                      |
|                      | of hydrostatic       |                      |
|                      | pressure behind it   |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check discharge pipe |                      |
|                      | endpoint             |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Must discharge 6+    |                      |
|                      | feet from            |                      |
|                      | foundation, sloping  |                      |
|                      | permanently away     |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Check sump cover:    |                      |
|                      | sealed or unsealed   |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | FEMA recommends      |                      |
|                      | sealed cover to      |                      |
|                      | prevent soil gas     |                      |
|                      | entry into living    |                      |
|                      | space                |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| ☐                    | Note battery backup  |                      |
|                      | unit: present, age,  |                      |
|                      | test status          |                      |
|                      |                      |                      |
|                      | Replace if battery   |                      |
|                      | age is unknown or    |                      |
|                      | greater than 3 years |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **MEASUREMENT**      | **RECORDED VALUE**   | **REFERENCE /        |
|                      |                      | THRESHOLD**          |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
| **Standing water     | \_\_                 | inches               |
| depth (if present)** | \_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_\_ |                      |
+----------------------+----------------------+----------------------+
